# Monsters A–Z

## Monsters: A

### Аболет

*Большой Аберрация, Принципиально-злой*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 17
- **Хиты:** 150 (20d10 + 40)
- **Speed:** 10 фт., Swim 40 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +3 (13)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   21   |   9    |   15   |   18   |   15   |   18   |
|   MOD    |   +5   |   -1   |   +2   |   +4   |   +2   |   +4   |
|   SAVE   |   +5   |   +3   |   +6   |   +8   |   +6   |   +4   |

- **Навыки:** История +12, Внимательность +10
- **Чувства:** darkvision 120 фт.; Passive Внимательность 20
- **Языки:** Глубинная речь; telepathy 120 фт.
- **ПО** 10 (ОО 5,900, or 7,200 in lair)

#### Traits

**_Amphibious._** The aboleth can breathe air and water.

**_Eldritch Restoration._** If destroyed, the aboleth gains a new body in 5d10 days, reviving with all its Хиты in the Far Realm or another location chosen by the DM.

**_Легендарное сопротивление (3/Day, or 4/Day in Lair)._** If the aboleth fails a saving throw, it can choose to succeed instead.

**_Mucus Cloud._** While underwater, the aboleth is surrounded by mucus. *Телосложение Saving Throw*: DC 14, each creature in a 5-foot Emanation originating from the aboleth at the end of the aboleth's turn. *Failure:* The target is cursed. Until the curse ends, the target's skin becomes slimy, the target can breathe air and water, and it can't regain Хиты unless it is underwater.
While the cursed creature is outside a body of water, the creature takes 6 (1d12) урон Кислота at the end of every 10 minutes unless moisture is applied to its skin before those minutes have passed.

**_Probing Телепатия._** If a creature the aboleth can see communicates telepathically with the aboleth, the aboleth learns the creature's greatest desires.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The aboleth makes two Tentacle attacks and uses either Consume Memories or Dominate Mind if available.

**_Tentacle._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +9, reach 15 фт. 12 (2d6 + 5) урон Дробящий. If the target is a Большой or smaller creature, it has the Схваченный condition (escape DC 14) from one of four tentacles.

**_Consume Memories._** *Интеллект Saving Throw*: DC 16, one creature within 30 feet that is Очарованный or Схваченный by the aboleth. *Failure:* 10 (3d6) урон Психический. *Success:* Half damage. *Failure or Success*: The aboleth gains the target's memories if the target is a Гуманоид and is reduced to 0 Хиты by this action.

**_Dominate Mind (2/Day)._** *Мудрость Saving Throw*: DC 16, one creature the aboleth can see within 30 feet. *Failure:* The target has the Очарованный condition until the aboleth dies or is on a different plane of existence from the target. While Очарованный, the target acts as an ally to the aboleth and is under its control while within 60 feet of it. In addition, the aboleth and the target can communicate telepathically with each other over any distance.
The target repeats the save whenever it takes damage as well as after every 24 hours it spends at least 1 mile away from the aboleth, ending the effect on itself on a success.

#### Legendary Действия

**_Lash._** The aboleth makes one Tentacle attack.

**_Psychic Drain._** If the aboleth has at least one creature Очарованный or Схваченный, it uses Consume Memories and regains 5 (1d10) Хиты.

### Анхег

*Большой Чудовище, Без мировоззрения*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 14
- **Хиты:** 45 (6d10 + 12)
- **Speed:** 30 фт., Burrow 10 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +0 (10)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   17   |   11   |   14   |   1    |   13   |   6    |
|   MOD    |   +3   |   +0   |   +2   |   -5   |   +1   |   -2   |
|   SAVE   |   +3   |   +0   |   +2   |   -5   |   +1   |   -2   |

- **Чувства:** darkvision 60 фт., tremorsense 60 фт.; Passive Внимательность 11
- **ПО** 2 (ОО 450; PB +2)

#### Traits

**_Tunneler._** The ankheg can рытьё through solid rock at half its Burrow Speed and leaves a 10-foot-diameter tunnel in its wake.

#### Действия

**_Bite._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +5 (with Advantage if the target is Схваченный by the ankheg), reach 5 фт. 10 (2d6 + 3) урон Рубящий plus 3 (1d6) урон Кислота. If the target is a Большой or smaller creature, it has the Схваченный condition (escape DC 13).

**_Acid Spray (Recharge 6)._** *Ловкость Saving Throw*: DC 12, each creature in a 30-foot-long, 5-foot-wide Line. *Failure:* 14 (4d6) урон Кислота. *Success:* Half damage.

### Убийца

*Маленький Гуманоид, Нейтральный*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 16
- **Хиты:** 97 (15d8 + 30)
- **Speed:** 30 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +10 (20)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   11   |   18   |   14   |   16   |   11   |   10   |
|   MOD    |   +0   |   +4   |   +2   |   +3   |   +0   |   +0   |
|   SAVE   |   +0   |   +7   |   +2   |   +6   |   +0   |   +0   |

- **Resistances:** Poison
- **Навыки:** Акробатика +7, Внимательность +6, Скрытность +10
- **Gear** Light Crossbow, Shortsword, Studded Leather Armor
- **Чувства:** Passive Внимательность 16
- **Языки:** Общий, Thieves' cant
- **ПО** 8 (ОО 3,900; PB +3)

#### Traits

**_Evasion._** If the assassin is subjected to an effect that allows it to make a Ловкость saving throw to take only half damage, the assassin instead takes no damage if it succeeds on the save and only half damage if it fails. It can't use this trait if it has the Недееспособный condition.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The assassin makes three attacks, using Shortsword or Light Crossbow in any combination.

**_Shortsword._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +7, reach 5 фт. 7 (1d6 + 4) урон Колющий plus 17 (5d6) урон Яд, and the target has the Отравленный condition until the start of the assassin's next turn.

**_Light Crossbow._** *Бросок дальнобойной атаки:* +7, range 80/320 фт. 8 (1d8 + 4) урон Колющий plus 21 (6d6) урон Яд.

#### Bonus Действия

**_Cunning Action._** The assassin takes the Dash, Disengage, or Hide action.

### Топорник

*Большой Чудовище, Без мировоззрения*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 11
- **Хиты:** 19 (3d10 + 3)
- **Speed:** 50 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +1 (11)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   14   |   12   |   12   |   2    |   10   |   5    |
|   MOD    |   +2   |   +1   |   +1   |   -4   |   +0   |   -3   |
|   SAVE   |   +2   |   +1   |   +1   |   -4   |   +0   |   -3   |

- **Чувства:** Passive Внимательность 10
- **ПО** 1/4 (ОО 50; PB +2)

#### Действия

**_Beak._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +4, reach 5 фт. 5 (1d6 + 2) урон Рубящий.

### Страж-азер

*Средний Элементаль, Принципиально-нейтральный*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 17
- **Хиты:** 39 (6d8 + 12)
- **Speed:** 30 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +1 (11)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   17   |   12   |   15   |   12   |   13   |   10   |
|   MOD    |   +3   |   +1   |   +2   |   +1   |   +1   |   +0   |
|   SAVE   |   +3   |   +1   |   +4   |   +1   |   +1   |   +0   |

- **Immunities:** Fire, Poison; Отравленный
- **Чувства:** Passive Внимательность 11
- **Языки:** Первичный (Ignan)
- **ПО** 2 (ОО 450; PB +2)

#### Traits

**_Fire Aura._** At the end of each of the azer's turns, each creature of the azer's choice in a 5-foot Emanation originating from the azer takes 5 (1d10) урон Огонь unless the azer has the Недееспособный condition.

**_Illumination._** The azer sheds Bright Light in a 10-foot radius and Dim Light for an additional 10 feet.

#### Действия

**_Burning Hammer._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +5, reach 5 фт. 8 (1d10 + 3) урон Дробящий plus 3 (1d6) урон Огонь.

## Monsters: Angels

### Дэва

*Средний Небожитель (Angel), Принципиально-добрый*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 17
- **Хиты:** 229 (27d8 + 108)
- **Speed:** 30 фт., Fly 90 фт. (hover)
- **Инициатива:** +4 (14)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   18   |   18   |   18   |   17   |   20   |   20   |
|   MOD    |   +4   |   +4   |   +4   |   +3   |   +5   |   +5   |
|   SAVE   |   +4   |   +4   |   +4   |   +3   |   +9   |   +9   |

- **Resistances:** Radiant
- **Immunities:** Очарованный, Истощение, Испуганный
- **Навыки:** Проницательность +9, Внимательность +9
- **Чувства:** darkvision 120 фт.; Passive Внимательность 19
- **Языки:** All; telepathy 120 фт.
- **ПО** 10 (ОО 5,900; PB +4)

#### Traits

**_Exalted Restoration._** If the deva dies outside Mount Celestia, its body disappears, and it gains a new body instantly, reviving with all its Хиты somewhere in Mount Celestia.

**_Magic Resistance._** The deva has Advantage on saving throws against spells and other magical effects.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The deva makes two Holy Mace attacks.

**_Holy Mace._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +8, reach 5 фт. 7 (1d6 + 4) урон Дробящий plus 18 (4d8) урон Излучение.

**_Использование заклинаний._** The deva casts one of the following spells, requiring no Material components and using Харизма as the spellcasting ability (spell save DC 17):

- **At Will:** *Обнаружение добра и зла*, *Изменение формы*
- **1e/Day Each:** *Причастие*, *Воскрешение мёртвых*

#### Bonus Действия

**_Divine Aid (2/Day)._** The deva casts *Лечение ран*, *Малое восстановление*, or *Снятие проклятия*, using the same spellcasting ability as Использование заклинаний.

### Планетар

*Большой Небожитель (Angel), Принципиально-добрый*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 19
- **Хиты:** 262 (21d10 + 147)
- **Speed:** 40 фт., Fly 120 фт. (hover)
- **Инициатива:** +10 (20)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   24   |   20   |   24   |   19   |   22   |   25   |
|   MOD    |   +7   |   +5   |   +7   |   +4   |   +6   |   +7   |
|   SAVE   |  +12   |   +5   |  +12   |   +4   |  +11   |  +12   |

- **Resistances:** Radiant
- **Immunities:** Очарованный, Истощение, Испуганный
- **Навыки:** Внимательность +11
- **Чувства:** truesight 120 фт.; Passive Внимательность 21
- **Языки:** All; telepathy 120 фт.
- **ПО** 16 (ОО 15,000; PB +5)

#### Traits

**_Divine Awareness._** The planetar knows if it hears a lie.

**_Exalted Restoration._** If the planetar dies outside Mount Celestia, its body disappears, and it gains a new body instantly, reviving with all its Хиты somewhere in Mount Celestia.

**_Magic Resistance._** The planetar has Advantage on saving throws against spells and other magical effects.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The planetar makes three Radiant Sword attacks or uses Holy Burst twice.

**_Radiant Sword._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +12, reach 10 фт. 14 (2d6 + 7) урон Рубящий plus 18 (4d8) урон Излучение.

**_Holy Burst._** *Ловкость Saving Throw*: DC 20, each enemy in a 20-foot-radius Sphere [Area of Effect]|ООHB|Sphere centered on a point the planetar can see within 120 feet. *Failure:* 24 (7d6) урон Излучение. *Success:* Half damage.

**_Использование заклинаний._** The planetar casts one of the following spells, requiring no Material components and using Харизма as spellcasting ability (spell save DC 20):

- **At Will:** *Обнаружение добра и зла*
- **1e/Day Each:** *Причастие*, *Власть над погодой*, *Рассеивание добра и зла*, *Воскрешение мёртвых*

#### Bonus Действия

**_Divine Aid (2/Day)._** The planetar casts *Лечение ран*, *Невидимость*, *Малое восстановление*, or *Снятие проклятия*, using the same spellcasting ability as Использование заклинаний.

### Солар

*Большой Небожитель (Angel), Принципиально-добрый*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 21
- **Хиты:** 297 (22d10 + 176)
- **Speed:** 50 фт., Fly 150 фт. (hover)
- **Инициатива:** +20 (30)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   26   |   22   |   26   |   25   |   25   |   30   |
|   MOD    |   +8   |   +6   |   +8   |   +7   |   +7   |  +10   |
|   SAVE   |   +8   |   +6   |   +8   |   +7   |   +7   |  +10   |

- **Immunities:** Poison, Radiant; Очарованный, Истощение, Испуганный, Отравленный
- **Навыки:** Внимательность +14
- **Чувства:** truesight 120 фт.; Passive Внимательность 24
- **Языки:** All; telepathy 120 фт.
- **ПО** 21 (ОО 33,000; PB +7)

#### Traits

**_Divine Awareness._** The solar knows if it hears a lie.

**_Exalted Restoration._** If the solar dies outside Mount Celestia, its body disappears, and it gains a new body instantly, reviving with all its Хиты somewhere in Mount Celestia.

**_Легендарное сопротивление (4/Day)._** If the solar fails a saving throw, it can choose to succeed instead.

**_Magic Resistance._** The solar has Advantage on saving throws against spells and other magical effects.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The solar makes two Flying Sword attacks. It can replace one attack with a use of Slaying Bow.

**_Flying Sword._** *Melee or Бросок дальнобойной атаки:* +15, reach 10 фт. or range 120 фт. 22 (4d6 + 8) урон Рубящий plus 36 (8d8) урон Излучение. *Hit or Miss.* The sword magically returns to the solar's hand or hovers within 5 feet of the solar immediately after a ranged attack.

**_Slaying Bow._** *Ловкость Saving Throw*: DC 21, one creature the solar can see within 600 feet. *Failure:* If the creature has 100 Хиты or fewer, it dies. It otherwise takes 24 (4d8 + 6) урон Колющий plus 36 (8d8) урон Излучение.

**_Использование заклинаний._** The solar casts one of the following spells, requiring no Material components and using Харизма as the spellcasting ability (spell save DC 25):

- **At Will:** *Обнаружение добра и зла*
- **1e/Day Each:** *Причастие*, *Власть над погодой*, *Рассеивание добра и зла*, *Воскрешение*

#### Bonus Действия

**_Divine Aid (3/Day)._** The solar casts *Лечение ран* (level 2 version), *Малое восстановление*, or *Снятие проклятия*, using the same spellcasting ability as Использование заклинаний.

#### Legendary Действия

**_Blinding Gaze._** *Телосложение Saving Throw*: DC 25, one creature the solar can see within 120 feet. *Failure:* The target has the Ослеплённый condition for 1 minute. *Failure or Success*: The solar can't take this action again until the start of its next turn.

**_Radiant Teleport._** The solar teleports up to 60 feet to an unoccupied space it can see. *Ловкость Saving Throw*: DC 25, each creature in a 10-foot Emanation originating from the solar at its destination space. *Failure:* 11 (2d10) урон Излучение. *Success:* Half damage.

## Monsters: Animated Objects

### Оживлённый доспех

*Средний Конструкт, Без мировоззрения*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 18
- **Хиты:** 33 (6d8 + 6)
- **Speed:** 25 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +2 (12)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   14   |   11   |   13   |   1    |   3    |   1    |
|   MOD    |   +2   |   +0   |   +1   |   -5   |   -4   |   -5   |
|   SAVE   |   +2   |   +0   |   +1   |   -5   |   -4   |   -5   |

- **Immunities:** Poison, Psychic; Очарованный, Оглохший, Истощение, Испуганный, Парализованный, Окаменевший, Отравленный
- **Чувства:** blindsight 60 фт.; Passive Внимательность 6
- **ПО** 1 (ОО 200; PB +2)

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The armor makes two Slam attacks.

**_Slam._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +4, reach 5 фт. 5 (1d6 + 2) урон Дробящий.

### Оживлённый ковёр-душитель

*Большой Конструкт, Без мировоззрения*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 12
- **Хиты:** 27 (5d10)
- **Speed:** 10 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +4 (14)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   17   |   14   |   10   |   1    |   3    |   1    |
|   MOD    |   +3   |   +2   |   +0   |   -5   |   -4   |   -5   |
|   SAVE   |   +3   |   +2   |   +0   |   -5   |   -4   |   -5   |

- **Immunities:** Poison, Psychic; Очарованный, Оглохший, Истощение, Испуганный, Парализованный, Окаменевший, Отравленный
- **Чувства:** blindsight 60 фт.; Passive Внимательность 6
- **ПО** 2 (ОО 450; PB +2)

#### Действия

**_Smother._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +5, reach 5 фт. 10 (2d6 + 3) урон Дробящий. If the target is a Средний or smaller creature, the rug can give it the Схваченный condition (escape DC 13) instead of dealing damage. Until the grapple ends, the target has the Ослеплённый and Опутанный conditions, is suffocating, and takes 10 (2d6 + 3) урон Дробящий at the start of each of its turns. The rug can smother only one creature at a time.
While grappling the target, the rug can't take this action, the rug halves the damage it takes (round down), and the target takes the same amount of damage.

## Monsters: Awakened Plants

### Пробуждённый куст

*Маленький Plant, Нейтральный*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 9
- **Хиты:** 10 (3d6)
- **Speed:** 20 фт.
- **Инициатива:** -1 (9)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   3    |   8    |   11   |   10   |   10   |   6    |
|   MOD    |   -4   |   -1   |   +0   |   +0   |   +0   |   -2   |
|   SAVE   |   -4   |   -1   |   +0   |   +0   |   +0   |   -2   |

- **Vulnerabilities:** Fire
- **Resistances:** Piercing
- **Чувства:** Passive Внимательность 10
- **Языки:** Общий plus one other language
- **ПО** 0 (ОО 0 or 10; PB +2)

#### Действия

**_Rake._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +1, reach 5 фт. 1 урон Рубящий.

### Пробуждённое дерево

*Огромный Plant, Нейтральный*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 13
- **Хиты:** 59 (7d12 + 14)
- **Speed:** 20 фт.
- **Инициатива:** -2 (8)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |

|  SCORE   |   23   |   16   |   18   |   7    |   14   |   12   |
|   MOD    |   +6   |   +3   |   +4   |   -2   |   +2   |   +1   |
|   SAVE   |   +6   |   +3   |   +4   |   -2   |   +2   |   +1   |

- **ПО** 11 (ОО 7,200; PB +4)

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The behir makes one Bite attack and uses Constrict.

**_Bite._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +10, reach 10 фт. 19 (2d12 + 6) урон Колющий plus 11 (2d10) урон Электричество.

**_Constrict._** *Сила Saving Throw*: DC 18, one Большой or smaller creature the behir can see within 5 feet. *Failure:* 28 (5d8 + 6) урон Дробящий. The target has the Схваченный condition (escape DC 16), and it has the Опутанный condition until the grapple ends.

**_Lightning Breath (Recharge 5-6)._** *Ловкость Saving Throw*: DC 16, each creature in a 90-foot-long, 5-foot-wide Line. *Failure:* 66 (12d10) урон Электричество. *Success:* Half damage.

#### Bonus Действия

**_Swallow._** *Ловкость Saving Throw*: DC 18, one Большой or smaller creature Схваченный by the behir (the behir can have only one creature swallowed at a time). *Failure:* The behir swallows the target, which is no longer Схваченный. While swallowed, a creature has the Ослеплённый and Опутанный conditions, has Cover|ООHB|Total Cover against attacks and other effects outside the behir, and takes 21 (6d6) урон Кислота at the start of each of the behir's turns.
If the behir takes 30 damage or more on a single turn from the swallowed creature, the behir must succeed on a DC 14 Телосложение saving throw at the end of that turn or regurgitate the creature, which falls in a space within 10 feet of the behir and has the Лежащий condition. If the behir dies, a swallowed creature is no longer Опутанный and can escape from the corpse by using 15 feet of movement, exiting Лежащий.

While the cloaker is attached, the target has the Ослеплённый condition, and the cloaker can't make Attach attacks against other targets. In addition, the cloaker halves the damage it takes (round down), and the target takes the same amount of damage.
The cloaker can detach itself by spending 5 feet of movement. The target or a creature within 5 feet of it can take an action to try to detach the cloaker, doing so by succeeding on a DC 14 Сила (Атлетика) check.

**_Tail._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +6, reach 10 фт. 8 (1d10 + 3) урон Рубящий.

#### Bonus Действия

**_Moan._** *Мудрость Saving Throw*: DC 13, each creature in a 60-foot Emanation originating from the cloaker. *Failure:* The target has the Испуганный condition until the end of the cloaker's next turn. *Success:* The target is immune to this cloaker's Moan for the next 24 hours.

**_Phantasms (Recharge after a Short or Long Rest)._** The cloaker casts the *Отражения* spell, requiring no spell components and using Мудрость as the spellcasting ability. The spell ends early if the cloaker starts or ends its turn in Bright Light.

**_Petrifying Bite._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +3, reach 5 фт. 3 (1d4 + 1) урон Колющий. If the target is a creature, it is subjected to the following effect. *Телосложение Saving Throw*: DC 11. *First Failure* The target has the Опутанный condition. The target repeats the save at the end of its next turn if it is still Опутанный, ending the effect on itself on a success. *Second Failure* The target has the Окаменевший condition, instead of the Опутанный condition, for 24 hours.

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   16   |   12   |   13   |   2    |   10   |   5    |

#### Действия

**_Crush._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +5, reach 5 фт. 6 (1d6 + 3) урон Дробящий, and the darkmantle attaches to the target. If the target is a Средний or smaller creature and the darkmantle had Advantage on the attack roll, it covers the target, which has the Ослеплённый condition and is suffocating while the darkmantle is attached in this way.
While attached to a target, the darkmantle can attack only the target but has Advantage on its attack rolls. Its Speed becomes 0, it can't benefit from any bonus to its Speed, and it moves with the target.
A creature can take an action to try to detach the darkmantle from itself, doing so with a successful DC 13 Сила (Атлетика) check. On its turn, the darkmantle can detach itself by using 5 feet of movement.

**_Darkness Aura (1/Day)._** Magical darkness fills a 15-foot Emanation originating from the darkmantle. This effect lasts while the darkmantle maintains Concentration on it, up to 10 minutes. Тёмное зрение can't penetrate this area, and no light can illuminate it.

### Джинн

*Большой Элементаль (Genie), Хаотично-добрый*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 17
- **Хиты:** 218 (19d10 + 114)
- **Speed:** 30 фт., Fly 90 фт. (hover)
- **Инициатива:** +2 (12)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   21   |   15   |   22   |   15   |   16   |   20   |
|   MOD    |   +5   |   +2   |   +6   |   +2   |   +3   |   +5   |
|   SAVE   |   +5   |   +6   |   +6   |   +2   |   +7   |   +5   |

- **Immunities:** Lightning, Thunder
- **Чувства:** darkvision 120 фт.; Passive Внимательность 13
- **Языки:** Первичный (Auran)
- **ПО** 11 (ОО 7,200; PB +4)

#### Traits

**_Elemental Restoration._** If the djinni dies outside the Элементаль Plane of Air, its body dissolves into mist, and it gains a new body in 1d4 days, reviving with all its Хиты somewhere on the Plane of Air.

**_Magic Resistance._** The djinni has Advantage on saving throws against spells and other magical effects.

**_Wishes._** The djinni has a 30 percent chance of knowing the *Исполнение желаний* spell. If the djinni knows it, the djinni can cast it only on behalf of a non-genie creature who communicates a wish in a way the djinni can understand. If the djinni casts the spell for the creature, the djinni suffers none of the spell's stress. Once the djinni has cast it three times, the djinni can't do so again for 365 days.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The djinni makes three attacks, using Storm Blade or Storm Bolt in any combination.

**_Storm Blade._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +9, reach 5 feet. 12 (2d6 + 5) урон Рубящий plus 7 (2d6) урон Электричество.

**_Storm Bolt._** *Бросок дальнобойной атаки:* +9, range 120 feet. 13 (3d8) урон Гром. If the target is a Большой or smaller creature, it has the Лежащий condition.

**_Create Whirlwind._** The djinni conjures a whirlwind at a point it can see within 120 feet. The whirlwind fills a 20-foot-radius, 60-foot-high Cylinder [Area of Effect]|ООHB|Cylinder centered on that point. The whirlwind lasts until the djinni's Concentration on it ends. The djinni can move the whirlwind up to 20 feet at the start of each of its turns.
Whenever the whirlwind enters a creature's space or a creature enters the whirlwind, that creature is subjected to the following effect. *Сила Saving Throw*: DC 17 (a creature makes this save only once per turn, and the djinni is unaffected). *Failure:* While in the whirlwind, the target has the Опутанный condition and moves with the whirlwind. At the start of each of its turns, the Опутанный target takes 21 (6d6) урон Гром. At the end of each of its turns, the target repeats the save, ending the effect on itself on a success.

**_Использование заклинаний._** The djinni casts one of the following spells, requiring no Material components and using Харизма as the spellcasting ability (spell save DC 17):

- **At Will:** *Обнаружение добра и зла*, *Обнаружение магии*
- **2e/Day Each:** *Сотворение пищи и воды*, *Языки*, *Хождение по ветру*
- **1e/Day Each:** *Сотворение*, *Газообразная форма*, *Невидимость*, *Высший образ*, *Переход между планами*

- **ПО** 19 (ОО 22,000; PB +6)

#### Traits

**_Death Throes._** The balor explodes when it dies. *Ловкость Saving Throw*: DC 20, each creature in a 30-foot Emanation originating from the balor. *Failure:* 31 (9d6) урон Огонь plus 31 (9d6) урон Силовое поле. *Success:* Half damage. *Failure or Success*: If the balor dies outside the Abyss, it gains a new body instantly, reviving with all its Хиты somewhere in the Abyss.

**_Fire Aura._** At the end of each of the balor's turns, each creature in a 5-foot Emanation originating from the balor takes 13 (3d8) урон Огонь.

**_Легендарное сопротивление (3/Day)._** If the balor fails a saving throw, it can choose to succeed instead.

**_Magic Resistance._** The balor has Advantage on saving throws against spells and other magical effects.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The balor makes one Flame Whip attack and one Lightning Blade attack.

**_Flame Whip._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +14, reach 30 фт. 18 (3d6 + 8) урон Силовое поле plus 17 (5d6) урон Огонь. If the target is a Огромный or smaller creature, the balor pulls the target up to 25 feet straight toward itself, and the target has the Лежащий condition.

**_Lightning Blade._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +14, reach 10 фт. 21 (3d8 + 8) урон Силовое поле plus 22 (4d10) урон Электричество, and the target can't take Реакции until the start of the balor's next turn.

#### Bonus Действия

**_Teleport._** The balor teleports itself or a willing demon within 10 feet of itself up to 60 feet to an unoccupied space the balor can see.

**_Chain._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +7, reach 10 фт. 11 (2d6 + 4) урон Рубящий. If the target is a Большой or smaller creature, it has the Схваченный condition (escape DC 14) from one of two chains, and it has the Опутанный condition until the grapple ends.

**_Conjure Инфернальный Chain._** The devil conjures a fiery chain to bind a creature. *Ловкость Saving Throw*: DC 15, one creature the devil can see within 60 feet. *Failure:* 9 (2d4 + 4) урон Огонь, and the target has the Опутанный condition until the end of the devil's next turn, at which point the chain disappears. If the target is Большой or smaller, the devil moves the target up to 30 feet straight toward itself. *Success:* The chain disappears.

|  SCORE   |   25   |   10   |   23   |   16   |   15   |   20   |
|   MOD    |   +7   |   +0   |   +6   |   +3   |   +2   |   +5   |
|   SAVE   |   +7   |   +5   |   +6   |   +3   |   +7   |   +5   |

- **Чувства:** blindsight 60 фт., darkvision 120 фт.; Passive Внимательность 22
- **Языки:** Общий, Драконий
- **ПО** 16 (ОО 15,000, or 18,000 in lair)

#### Traits

**_Легендарное сопротивление (3/Day, or 4/Day in Lair)._** If the dragon fails a saving throw, it can choose to succeed instead.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The dragon makes three Rend attacks. It can replace one attack with a use of Использование заклинаний to cast *Дребезги*.

**_Rend._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +12, reach 10 фт. 16 (2d8 + 7) урон Рубящий plus 5 (1d10) урон Электричество.

**_Lightning Breath (Recharge 5-6)._** *Ловкость Saving Throw*: DC 19, each creature in a 90-foot-long, 5-foot-wide Line. *Failure:* 60 (11d10) урон Электричество. *Success:* Half damage.

**_Использование заклинаний._** The dragon casts one of the following spells, requiring no Material components and using Харизма as the spellcasting ability (spell save DC 18):

- **At Will:** *Обнаружение магии*, *Невидимость*, *Волшебная рука*, *Дребезги*
- **1e/Day Each:** *Наблюдение*, *Послание*

#### Legendary Действия

**_Cloaked Flight._** The dragon uses Использование заклинаний to cast *Невидимость* on itself, and it can fly up to half its Fly Speed. The dragon can't take this action again until the start of its next turn.

**_Sonic Boom._** The dragon uses Использование заклинаний to cast *Дребезги*. The dragon can't take this action again until the start of its next turn.

**_Tail Swipe._** The dragon makes one Rend attack.

**_Rend._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +12, reach 10 фт. 16 (2d8 + 7) урон Рубящий plus 5 (1d10) урон Электричество.

**_Lightning Breath (Recharge 5-6)._** *Ловкость Saving Throw*: DC 19, each creature in a 90-foot-long, 5-foot-wide Line. *Failure:* 55 (10d10) урон Электричество. *Success:* Half damage.

**_Repulsion Breath._** *Сила Saving Throw*: DC 19, each creature in a 30-foot Cone. *Failure:* The target is pushed up to 60 feet straight away from the dragon and has the Лежащий condition.

**_Использование заклинаний._** The dragon casts one of the following spells, requiring no Material components and using Харизма as the spellcasting ability (spell save DC 17, +10 to hit with spell attacks):

- **At Will:** *Обнаружение магии*, *Направляющий снаряд*, *Изменение формы*, *Разговор с животными*, *Тауматургия*
- **1e/Day Each:** *Обнаружение мыслей*, *Дыхание под водой*

#### Legendary Действия

**_Guiding Light._** The dragon uses Использование заклинаний to cast *Направляющий снаряд* (level 2 version).

**_Pounce._** The dragon moves up to half its Speed, and it makes one Rend attack.

**_Thunderclap._** *Телосложение Saving Throw*: DC 17, each creature in a 20-foot-radius Sphere [Area of Effect]|ООHB|Sphere centered on a point the dragon can see within 90 feet. *Failure:* 10 (3d6) урон Гром, and the target has the Оглохший condition until the end of its next turn.

**_Rend._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +17 to hit, reach 15 фт. 19 (2d8 + 10) урон Рубящий plus 9 (2d8) урон Огонь.

**_Fire Breath (Recharge 5-6)._** *Ловкость Saving Throw*: DC 24, each creature in a 90-foot Cone. *Failure:* 71 (13d10) урон Огонь. *Success:* Half damage.

**_Weakening Breath._** *Сила Saving Throw*: DC 24, each creature that isn't currently affected by this breath in a 90-foot Cone. *Failure:* The target has Disadvantage on Сила-based D20 Test and subtracts 5 (1d10) from its damage rolls. It repeats the save at the end of each of its turns, ending the effect on itself on a success. After 1 minute, it succeeds automatically.

**_Использование заклинаний._** The dragon casts one of the following spells, requiring no Material components and using Харизма as the spellcasting ability (spell save DC 24, +16 to hit with spell attacks):

- **At Will:** *Обнаружение магии*, *Направляющий снаряд*, *Изменение формы*
- **1e/Day Each:** *Небесный огонь*, *Слово возврата*, *Зона правды*

#### Legendary Действия

**_Banish._** *Харизма Saving Throw*: DC 24, one creature the dragon can see within 120 feet. *Failure:* 24 (7d6) урон Силовое поле, and the target has the Недееспособный condition and is transported to a harmless demiplane until the start of the dragon's next turn, at which point it reappears in an unoccupied space of the dragon's choice within 120 feet of the dragon. *Failure or Success*: The dragon can't take this action again until the start of its next turn.

**_Guiding Light._** The dragon uses Использование заклинаний to cast *Направляющий снаряд* (level 4 version).

**_Pounce._** The dragon moves up to half its Speed, and it makes one Rend attack.

|   SAVE   |   +8   |   +5   |   +7   |   +3   |   +6   |   +6   |

- **Immunities:** Cold
- **Навыки:** История +8, Внимательность +11, Скрытность +5
- **Чувства:** blindsight 60 фт., darkvision 120 фт.; Passive Внимательность 21
- **Языки:** Общий, Драконий
- **ПО** 16 (ОО 15,000, or 18,000 in lair)

#### Traits

**_Легендарное сопротивление (3/Day, or 4/Day in Lair)._** If the dragon fails a saving throw, it can choose to succeed instead.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The dragon makes three Rend attacks. It can replace one attack with a use of (A) Paralyzing Breath or (B) Использование заклинаний to cast *Ледяной нож*.

**_Rend._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +13, reach 10 фт. 17 (2d8 + 8) урон Рубящий plus 4 (1d8) урон Холод.

**_Cold Breath (Recharge 5-6)._** *Телосложение Saving Throw*: DC 20, each creature in a 60-foot Cone. *Failure:* 54 (12d8) урон Холод. *Success:* Half damage.

**_Paralyzing Breath._** *Телосложение Saving Throw*: DC 20, each creature in a 60-foot Cone. *First Failure* The target has the Недееспособный condition until the end of its next turn, when it repeats the save. *Second Failure* The target has the Парализованный condition, and it repeats the save at the end of each of its turns, ending the effect on itself on a success. After 1 minute, it succeeds automatically.

**_Использование заклинаний._** The dragon casts one of the following spells, requiring no Material components and using Харизма as the spellcasting ability (spell save DC 19, +11 to hit with spell attacks):

- **At Will:** *Обнаружение магии*, *Удержание чудовища*, *Ледяной нож*, *Изменение формы*
- **1e/Day Each:** *Град*, *Зона правды*

#### Legendary Действия

**_Chill._** The dragon uses Использование заклинаний to cast *Удержание чудовища*. The dragon can't take this action again until the start of its next turn.

**_Cold Gale._** *Ловкость Saving Throw*: DC 19, each creature in a 60-foot-long, 10-foot-wide Line. *Failure:* 14 (4d6) урон Холод, and the target is pushed up to 30 feet straight away from the dragon. *Success:* Half damage only. *Failure or Success*: The dragon can't take this action again until the start of its next turn.

**_Pounce._** The dragon moves up to half its Speed, and it makes one Rend attack.

- **Хиты:** 212 (17d10 + 119)
- **Speed:** 40 фт., Fly 60 фт. (hover)
- **Инициатива:** +1 (11)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   22   |   12   |   24   |   16   |   15   |   19   |
|   MOD    |   +6   |   +1   |   +7   |   +3   |   +2   |   +4   |
|   SAVE   |   +6   |   +1   |   +7   |   +3   |   +6   |   +8   |

- **Чувства:** darkvision 120 фт.; Passive Внимательность 12
- **Языки:** Первичный (Ignan)
- **ПО** 11 (ОО 7,200; PB +4)

#### Traits

**_Elemental Restoration._** If the efreeti dies outside the Элементаль Plane of Fire, its body dissolves into ash, and it gains a new body in 1d4 days, reviving with all its Хиты somewhere on the Plane of Fire.

**_Magic Resistance._** The efreeti has Advantage on saving throws against spells and other magical effects.

**_Wishes._** The efreeti has a 30 percent chance of knowing the *Исполнение желаний* spell. If the efreeti knows it, the efreeti can cast it only on behalf of a non-genie creature who communicates a wish in a way the efreeti can understand. If the efreeti casts the spell for the creature, the efreeti suffers none of the spell's stress. Once the efreeti has cast it three times, the efreeti can't do so again for 365 days.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The efreeti makes three attacks, using Heated Blade or Hurl Flame in any combination.

**_Heated Blade._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +10, reach 5 фт. 13 (2d6 + 6) урон Рубящий plus 13 (2d12) урон Огонь.

**_Hurl Flame._** *Бросок дальнобойной атаки:* +8, range 120 фт. 24 (7d6) урон Огонь.

**_Использование заклинаний._** The efreeti casts one of the following spells, requiring no Material components and using Харизма as the spellcasting ability (spell save DC 16):

- **At Will:** *Обнаружение магии*, *Стихийная магия*
- **1e/Day Each:** *Газообразная форма*, *Невидимость*, *Высший образ*, *Переход между планами*, *Языки*, *Стена огня*

**_Earth Glide._** The elemental can рытьё through nonmagical, unworked earth and stone. While doing so, the elemental doesn't disturb the material it moves through.

**_Siege Monster._** The elemental deals double damage to objects and structures.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The elemental makes two attacks, using Slam or Rock Launch in any combination.

**_Slam._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +8, reach 10 фт. 14 (2d8 + 5) урон Дробящий.

**_Rock Launch._** *Бросок дальнобойной атаки:* +8, range 60 фт. 8 (1d6 + 5) урон Дробящий. If the target is a Большой or smaller creature, it has the Лежащий condition.

### Огненный элементаль

*Большой Элементаль, Нейтральный*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 13
- **Хиты:** 93 (11d10 + 33)
- **Speed:** 50 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +3 (13)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   10   |   17   |   16   |   6    |   10   |   7    |

|   SAVE   |   +0   |   +3   |   +3   |   -2   |   +0   |   -2   |

- **Resistances:** Bludgeoning, Piercing, Slashing

- **Чувства:** darkvision 60 фт.; Passive Внимательность 10
- **Языки:** Первичный (Ignan)
- **ПО** 5 (ОО 1,800; PB +3)

#### Traits

**_Fire Aura._** At the end of each of the elemental's turns, each creature in a 10-foot Emanation originating from the elemental takes 5 (1d10) урон Огонь. Creatures and flammable objects in the Emanation start Hitazard burning.

**_Fire Form._** The elemental can move through a space as narrow as 1 inch without expending extra movement to do so, and it can enter a creature's space and stop there. The first time it enters a creature's space on a turn, that creature takes 5 (1d10) урон Огонь.

**_Illumination._** The elemental sheds Bright Light in a 30-foot radius and Dim Light for an additional 30 feet.

**_Water Susceptibility._** The elemental takes 3 (1d6) урон Холод for every 5 feet the elemental moves in water or for every gallon of water splashed on it.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The elemental makes two Burn attacks.

**_Burn._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +6, reach 5 фт. 10 (2d6 + 3) урон Огонь. If the target is a creature or a flammable object, it starts burning.

### Водяной элементаль

*Большой Элементаль, Нейтральный*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 14
- **Хиты:** 114 (12d10 + 48)
- **Speed:** 30 фт., Swim 90 фт.

**_Whelm (Recharge 4-6)._** *Сила Saving Throw*: DC 15, each creature in the elemental's space. *Failure:* 22 (4d8 + 4) урон Дробящий. If the target is a Большой or smaller creature, it has the Схваченный condition (escape DC 14). Until the grapple ends, the target has the Опутанный condition, is suffocating unless it can breathe water, and takes 9 (2d8) урон Дробящий at the start of each of the elemental's turns. The elemental can grapple one Большой creature or up to two Средний or smaller creatures at a time with Whelm. As an action, a creature within 5 feet of the elemental can pull a creature out of it by succeeding on a DC 14 Сила (Атлетика) check. *Success:* Half damage only.

**_Horrific Visage._** *Мудрость Saving Throw*: DC 13, each creature in a 60-foot Cone that can see the ghost and isn't an Нежить. *Failure:* 10 (2d6 + 3) урон Психический, and the target has the Испуганный condition until the start of the ghost's next turn. *Success:* The target is immune to this ghost's Horrific Visage for 24 hours.

**_Possession (Recharge 6)._** *Харизма Saving Throw*: DC 13, one Гуманоид the ghost can see within 5 feet. *Failure:* The target is possessed by the ghost; the ghost disappears, and the target has the Недееспособный condition and loses control of its body. The ghost now controls the body, but the target retains awareness. The ghost can't be targeted by any attack, spell, or other effect, except ones that specifically target Нежить. The ghost's game statistics are the same, except it uses the possessed target's Speed, as well as the target's Сила, Ловкость, and Телосложение modifiers.
The possession lasts until the body drops to 0 Хиты or the ghost leaves as a Bonus Action. When the possession ends, the ghost appears in an unoccupied space within 5 feet of the target, and the target is immune to this ghost's Possession for 24 hours. *Success:* The target is immune to this ghost's Possession for 24 hours.

**_Etherealness._** The ghost casts the *Эфирность* spell, requiring no spell components and using Харизма as the spellcasting ability. The ghost is visible on the Material Plane while on the Border Ethereal and vice versa, but it can't affect or be affected by anything on the other plane.

- **At Will:** *Эфирность*

## Monsters: Golems

### Глиняный голем

*Большой Конструкт, Без мировоззрения*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 14
- **Хиты:** 123 (13d10 + 52)
- **Speed:** 20 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +3 (13)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   20   |   9    |   18   |   3    |   8    |   1    |
|   MOD    |   +5   |   -1   |   +4   |   -4   |   -1   |   -5   |
|   SAVE   |   +5   |   -1   |   +4   |   -4   |   -1   |   -5   |

- **Resistances:** Bludgeoning, Piercing, Slashing
- **Immunities:** Acid, Poison, Psychic; Очарованный, Истощение, Испуганный, Парализованный, Окаменевший, Отравленный
- **Чувства:** darkvision 60 фт.; Passive Внимательность 9
- **Языки:** Общий plus one other language
- **ПО** 9 (ОО 5,000; PB +4)

#### Traits

**_Acid Absorption._** Whenever the golem is subjected to урон Кислота, it takes no damage and instead regains a number of Хиты equal to the урон Кислота dealt.

**_Berserk._** Whenever the golem starts its turn Bloodied, roll 1d6. On a 6, the golem goes berserk. On each of its turns while berserk, the golem attacks the nearest creature it can see. If no creature is near enough to move to and attack, the golem attacks an object. Once the golem goes berserk, it continues to be berserk until it is destroyed or it is no longer Bloodied.

**_Immutable Form._** The golem can't shape-shiфт.

**_Magic Resistance._** The golem has Advantage on saving throws against spells and other magical effects.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The golem makes two Slam attacks, or it makes three Slam attacks if it used Hasten this turn.

**_Slam._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +9, reach 5 фт. 10 (1d10 + 5) урон Дробящий plus 6 (1d12) урон Кислота, and the target's Hit Point maximum decreases by an amount equal to the урон Кислота taken.

#### Bonus Действия

**_Hasten (Recharge 5-6)._** The golem takes the Dash and Disengage actions.

### Голем из плоти

*Средний Конструкт, Нейтральный*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 9
- **Хиты:** 127 (15d8 + 60)
- **Speed:** 30 фт.
- **Инициатива:** -1 (9)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   19   |   9    |   18   |   6    |   10   |   5    |
|   MOD    |   +4   |   -1   |   +4   |   -2   |   +0   |   -3   |
|   SAVE   |   +4   |   -1   |   +4   |   -2   |   +0   |   -3   |

- **Immunities:** Lightning, Poison; Очарованный, Истощение, Испуганный, Парализованный, Окаменевший, Отравленный
- **Чувства:** darkvision 60 фт.; Passive Внимательность 10
- **Языки:** Understands Общий plus one other language но не может говорить
- **ПО** 5 (ОО 1,800; PB +3)

#### Traits

**_Aversion to Fire._** If the golem takes урон Огонь, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls and ability checks until the end of its next turn.

**_Berserk._** Whenever the golem starts its turn Bloodied, roll 1d6. On a 6, the golem goes berserk. On each of its turns while berserk, the golem attacks the nearest creature it can see. If no creature is near enough to move to and attack, the golem attacks an object. Once the golem goes berserk, it remains so until it is destroyed or it is no longer Bloodied.
The golem's creator, if within 60 feet of the berserk golem, can try to calm it by taking an action to make a DC 15 Харизма (Убеждение) check; the golem must be able to hear its creator. If this check succeeds, the golem ceases being berserk until the start of its next turn, at which point it resumes rolling for the Berserk trait again if it is still Bloodied.

**_Immutable Form._** The golem can't shape-shiфт.

**_Lightning Absorption._** Whenever the golem is subjected to урон Электричество, it regains a number of Хиты equal to the урон Электричество dealt.

**_Magic Resistance._** The golem has Advantage on saving throws against spells and other magical effects.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The golem makes two Slam attacks.

**_Slam._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +7, reach 5 фт. 13 (2d8 + 4) урон Дробящий plus 4 (1d8) урон Электричество.

**_Luring Song._** The harpy sings a magical melody, which lasts until the harpy's Concentration ends on it. *Мудрость Saving Throw*: DC 11, each Гуманоид and Великаний in a 300-foot Emanation originating from the harpy when the song starts. *Failure:* The target has the Очарованный condition until the song ends and repeats the save at the end of each of its turns. While Очарованный, the target has the Недееспособный condition and ignores the Luring Song of other harpies. If the target is more than 5 feet from the harpy, the target moves on its turn toward the harpy by the most direct route, trying to get within 5 feet of the harpy. It doesn't avoid Opportunity Attacks; however, before moving into damaging terrain (such as lava or a pit) and whenever it takes damage from a source other than the harpy, the target repeats the save. *Success:* The target is immune to this harpy's Luring Song for 24 hours.

- **Хиты:** 184 (16d12 + 80)
- **Speed:** 40 фт., Swim 40 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +4 (14)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   20   |   12   |   20   |   2    |   10   |   7    |

|   SAVE   |   +5   |   +1   |   +5   |   -4   |   +0   |   -2   |

**_Hold Breath._** The hydra can hold its breath for 1 hour.

**_Multiple Heads._** The hydra has five heads. Whenever the hydra takes 25 damage or more on a single turn, one of its heads dies. The hydra dies if all its heads are dead. At the end of each of its turns when it has at least one living head, the hydra grows two heads for each of its heads that died since its last turn, unless it has taken урон Огонь since its last turn. The hydra regains 20 Хиты when it grows new heads.

**_Reactive Heads._** For each head the hydra has beyond one, it gets an extra Reaction that can be used only for Opportunity Attacks.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The hydra makes as many Bite attacks as it has heads.

**_Bite._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +8, reach 10 фт. 10 (1d10 + 5) урон Колющий.

### Ночная карга

*Средний Исчадие, Нейтральный Evil*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 17
- **Хиты:** 112 (15d8 + 45)
- **Speed:** 30 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +5 (15)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   18   |   15   |   16   |   16   |   14   |   16   |
|   MOD    |   +4   |   +2   |   +3   |   +3   |   +2   |   +3   |
|   SAVE   |   +4   |   +2   |   +3   |   +3   |   +2   |   +3   |

- **Resistances:** Cold, Fire

- **ПО** 5 (ОО 1,800; PB +3)

#### Traits

**_Magic Resistance._** The hag has Advantage on saving throws against spells and other magical effects.

**_Soul Bag._** The hag has a soul bag. While holding or carrying the bag, the hag can use its Nightmare Haunting action.
The bag has AC 15, HP 20, and Resistance to all damage. The bag turns to dust if reduced to 0 Хиты. If the bag is destroyed, any souls the bag is holding are released. The hag can create a new bag after 7 days.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The hag makes two Claw attacks.

**_Claw._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +7, reach 5 фт. 13 (2d8 + 4) урон Рубящий.

**_Использование заклинаний._** The hag casts one of the following spells, requiring no Material components and using Интеллект as the spellcasting ability (spell save DC 14):

- **At Will:** *Обнаружение магии*, *Эфирность*, *Магическая стрела*
- **2e/Day Each:** *Призрачный убийца*, *Переход между планами*
**_Nightmare Haunting (1/Day; Requires Soul Bag)._** While on the Ethereal Plane, the hag casts *Сон*, using the same spellcasting ability as Использование заклинаний. Only the hag can serve as the spell's messenger, and the target must be a creature the hag can see on the Material Plane. The spell fails and is wasted if the target is under the effect of the *Защита от добра и зла* spell or within a *Магический круг* spell.
If the target takes damage from the *Сон* spell, the target's Hit Point maximum decreases by an amount equal to that damage. If the spell kills the target, its soul is trapped in the hag's soul bag, and the target can't be raised from the dead until its soul is released.

- **At Will:**
- **1/Day Each:** *Сон*, *Защита от добра и зла*, *Магический круг*

#### Bonus Действия

**_Shape-Shiфт._** The hag shape-shifts into a Маленький or Средний Гуманоид, or it returns to its true form. Other than its size, its game statistics are the same in each form. Any equipment it is wearing or carrying isn't transformed.

- **Хиты:** 52 (7d8 + 21)

Otherwise, the target takes 18 (4d8) урон Психический.

- **Хиты:** 481 (26d20 + 208)
- **Speed:** 30 фт., Swim 120 фт.

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|

- **Навыки:** История +13, Внимательность +11
- **Чувства:** truesight 120 фт.; Passive Внимательность 21
- **Языки:** Understands Бездны, Небожитель, Инфернальный, And Первичный но не может говорить; telepathy 120 фт.
- **ПО** 23 (ОО 50,000, or 62,000 in lair)

#### Traits

**_Amphibious._** The kraken can breathe air and water.

**_Легендарное сопротивление (4/Day, or 5/Day in Lair)._** If the kraken fails a saving throw, it can choose to succeed instead.

**_Siege Monster._** The kraken deals double damage to objects and structures.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The kraken makes two Tentacle attacks and uses Fling, Lightning Strike, or Swallow.

**_Tentacle._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +17, reach 30 фт. 24 (4d6 + 10) урон Дробящий. The target has the Схваченный condition (escape DC 20) from one of ten tentacles, and it has the Опутанный condition until the grapple ends.

**_Fling._** The kraken throws a Большой or smaller creature Схваченный by it to a space it can see within 60 feet of itself that isn't in the air. *Ловкость Saving Throw*: DC 25, the creature thrown and each creature in the destination space. *Failure:* 18 (4d8) урон Дробящий, and the target has the Лежащий condition. *Success:* Half damage only.

**_Lightning Strike._** *Ловкость Saving Throw*: DC 23, one creature the kraken can see within 120 feet. *Failure:* 33 (6d10) урон Электричество. *Success:* Half damage.

**_Swallow._** *Ловкость Saving Throw*: DC 25, one creature Схваченный by the kraken (it can have up to four creatures swallowed at a time). *Failure:* 23 (3d8 + 10) урон Колющий. If the target is Большой or smaller, it is swallowed and no longer Схваченный. A swallowed creature has the Опутанный condition, has Cover|ООHB|Total Cover against attacks and other effects outside the kraken, and takes 24 (7d6) урон Кислота at the start of each of its turns.
If the kraken takes 50 damage or more on a single turn from a creature inside it, the kraken must succeed on a DC 25 Телосложение saving throw at the end of that turn or regurgitate all swallowed creatures, each of which falls in a space within 10 feet of the kraken with the Лежащий condition. If the kraken dies, any swallowed creature no longer has the Опутанный condition and can escape from the corpse using 15 feet of movement, exiting Лежащий.

#### Legendary Действия

**_Storm Bolt._** The kraken uses Lightning Strike.

**_Toxic Ink._** *Телосложение Saving Throw*: DC 23, each creature in a 15-foot Emanation originating from the kraken while it is underwater. *Failure:* The target has the Ослеплённый and Отравленный conditions until the end of the kraken's next turn. The kraken then moves up to its Speed. *Failure or Success*: The kraken can't take this action again until the start of its next turn.

#### Реакции

**_Protective Magic._** The lich casts *Контрзаклинание* or *Щит* in response to the spell's trigger, using the same spellcasting ability as Использование заклинаний.

#### Legendary Действия

**_Deathly Teleport._** The lich teleports up to 60 feet to an unoccupied space it can see, and each creature within 10 feet of the space it left takes 11 (2d10) урон Некротический.

**_Disrupt Life._** *Телосложение Saving Throw*: DC 20, each creature that isn't an Нежить in a 20-foot Emanation originating from the lich. *Failure:* 31 (9d6) урон Некротический. *Success:* Half damage. *Failure or Success*: The lich can't take this action again until the start of its next turn.

**_Frightening Gaze._** The lich casts *Страх*, using the same spellcasting ability as Использование заклинаний. The lich can't take this action again until the start of its next turn.

#### Bonus Действия

**_Shape-Shiфт._** The weretiger shape-shifts into a Большой tiger-humanoid hybrid or a Большой tiger, or it returns to its true humanoid form. Its game statistics, other than its size, are the same in each form. Any equipment it is wearing or carrying isn't transformed.

## Monsters: Mummies

### Мумия

*Маленький Нежить, Принципиально-злой*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 11
- **Хиты:** 58 (9d8 + 18)
- **Speed:** 20 фт.
- **Инициатива:** -1 (9)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   16   |   8    |   15   |   6    |   12   |   12   |
|   MOD    |   +3   |   -1   |   +2   |   -2   |   +1   |   +1   |
|   SAVE   |   +3   |   -1   |   +2   |   -2   |   +3   |   +1   |

- **Vulnerabilities:** Fire
- **Immunities:** Necrotic, Poison; Очарованный, Истощение, Испуганный, Парализованный, Отравленный
- **Чувства:** darkvision 60 фт.; Passive Внимательность 11
- **Языки:** Общий plus two other languages
- **ПО** 3 (ОО 700; PB +2)

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The mummy makes two Rotting Fist attacks and uses Dreadful Glare.

**_Rotting Fist._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +5, reach 5 фт. 8 (1d10 + 3) урон Дробящий plus 10 (3d6) урон Некротический. If the target is a creature, it is cursed. While cursed, the target can't regain Хиты, its Hit Point maximum doesn't return to normal when finishing a Long Rest, and its Hit Point maximum decreases by 10 (3d6) every 24 hours that elapse. A creature dies and turns to dust if reduced to 0 Хиты by this attack.

**_Dreadful Glare._** *Мудрость Saving Throw*: DC 11, one creature the mummy can see within 60 feet. *Failure:* The target has the Испуганный condition until the end of the mummy's next turn. *Success:* The target is immune to this mummy's Dreadful Glare for 24 hours.

### Повелитель мумий

*Маленький Нежить, Принципиально-злой*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 17
- **Хиты:** 187 (25d8 + 75)
- **Speed:** 30 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +4 (14)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   18   |   10   |   17   |   11   |   19   |   16   |
|   MOD    |   +4   |   +0   |   +3   |   +0   |   +4   |   +3   |
|   SAVE   |   +4   |   +0   |   +3   |   +5   |   +9   |   +3   |

- **Vulnerabilities:** Fire
- **Immunities:** Necrotic, Poison; Очарованный, Истощение, Испуганный, Парализованный, Отравленный
- **Навыки:** История +5, Внимательность +9, Религия +5
- **Чувства:** truesight 60 фт.; Passive Внимательность 19
- **Языки:** Общий plus three other languages
- **ПО** 15 (ОО 13,000, or 15,000 in lair)

#### Traits

**_Легендарное сопротивление (3/Day, or 4/Day in Lair)._** If the mummy fails a saving throw, it can choose to succeed instead.

**_Magic Resistance._** The mummy has Advantage on saving throws against spells and other magical effects.

**_Undead Restoration._** If destroyed, the mummy gains a new body in 24 hours if its heart is intact, reviving with all its Хиты. The new body appears in an unoccupied space within the mummy's lair. The heart is a Крошечный object that has AC 17, HP 10, and Immunity to all damage except Fire.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The mummy makes one Rotting Fist or Channel Negative Energy attack, and it uses Dreadful Glare.

**_Rotting Fist._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +9, reach 5 фт. 15 (2d10 + 4) урон Дробящий plus 10 (3d6) урон Некротический. If the target is a creature, it is cursed. While cursed, the target can't regain Хиты, it gains no benefit from finishing a Long Rest, and its Hit Point maximum decreases by 10 (3d6) every 24 hours that elapse. A creature dies and turns to dust if reduced to 0 Хиты by this attack.

**_Channel Negative Energy._** *Бросок дальнобойной атаки:* +9, range 60 фт. 25 (6d6 + 4) урон Некротический.

**_Dreadful Glare._** *Мудрость Saving Throw*: DC 17, one creature the mummy can see within 60 feet. *Failure:* 25 (6d6 + 4) урон Психический, and the target has the Парализованный condition until the end of the mummy's next turn.

**_Использование заклинаний._** The mummy casts one of the following spells, requiring no Material components and using Мудрость as the spellcasting ability (spell save DC 17, +9 to hit with spell attacks):

- **At Will:** *Рассеивание магии*, *Тауматургия*
- **1e/Day Each:** *Оживление мёртвых*, *Нанесение вреда*, *Нашествие насекомых*

#### Legendary Действия

**_Glare._** The mummy uses Dreadful Glare. The mummy can't take this action again until the start of its next turn.

**_Necrotic Strike._** The mummy makes one Rotting Fist or Channel Negative Energy attack.

**_Dread Command._** The mummy casts *Приказ* (level 2 version), using the same spellcasting ability as Использование заклинаний. The mummy can't take this action again until the start of its next turn.

### Отиуг

*Большой Аберрация, Нейтральный*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 14
- **Хиты:** 104 (11d10 + 44)
- **Speed:** 30 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +0 (10)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   16   |   11   |   19   |   6    |   13   |   6    |
|   MOD    |   +3   |   +0   |   +4   |   -2   |   +1   |   -2   |
|   SAVE   |   +3   |   +0   |   +7   |   -2   |   +1   |   -2   |

- **Чувства:** darkvision 120 фт.; Passive Внимательность 11
- **Языки:** Otyugh; telepathy 120 фт. (doesn't allow the receiving creature to respond telepathically)
- **ПО** 5 (ОО 1,800; PB +3)

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The otyugh makes one Bite attack and two Tentacle attacks.

**_Bite._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +6, reach 5 фт. 12 (2d8 + 3) урон Колющий, and the target has the Отравленный condition. Whenever the Отравленный target finishes a Long Rest, it is subjected to the following effect. *Телосложение Saving Throw*: DC 15. *Failure:* The target's Hit Point maximum decreases by 5 (1d10) and doesn't return to normal until the Отравленный condition ends on the target. *Success:* The Отравленный condition ends.

**_Tentacle._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +6, reach 10 фт. 12 (2d8 + 3) урон Колющий. If the target is a Средний or smaller creature, it has the Схваченный condition (escape DC 13) from one of two tentacles.

**_Tentacle Slam._** *Телосложение Saving Throw*: DC 14, each creature Схваченный by the otyugh. *Failure:* 16 (3d8 + 3) урон Дробящий, and the target has the Ошеломлённый condition until the start of the otyugh's next turn. *Success:* Half damage only.

## Monsters: Oozes

### Чёрная слизь

*Большой Слизь, Без мировоззрения*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 7
- **Хиты:** 68 (8d10 + 24)
- **Speed:** 20 фт., Climb 20 фт.
- **Инициатива:** -3 (7)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   16   |   5    |   16   |   1    |   6    |   1    |
|   MOD    |   +3   |   -3   |   +3   |   -5   |   -2   |   -5   |
|   SAVE   |   +3   |   -3   |   +3   |   -5   |   -2   |   -5   |

- **Immunities:** Acid, Cold, Lightning, Slashing; Очарованный, Оглохший, Истощение, Испуганный, Схваченный, Лежащий, Опутанный
- **Чувства:** blindsight 60 фт.; Passive Внимательность 8
- **ПО** 4 (ОО 1,100; PB +2)

#### Traits

**_Amorphous._** The pudding can move through a space as narrow as 1 inch without expending extra movement to do so.

**_Corrosive Form._** A creature that hits the pudding with a melee attack roll takes 4 (1d8) урон Кислота. Nonmagical ammunition is destroyed immediately after hitting the pudding and dealing any damage. Any nonmagical weapon takes a cumulative -1 penalty to attack rolls immediately after dealing damage to the pudding and coming into contact with it. The weapon is destroyed if the penalty reaches -5. The penalty can be removed by casting the *Починка* spell on the weapon.
In 1 minute, the pudding can eat through 2 feet of nonmagical wood or metal.

**_Spider Climb._** The pudding can climb difficult surfaces, including along ceilings, without needing to make an ability check.

#### Действия

**_Dissolving Pseudopod._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +5, reach 10 фт. 17 (4d6 + 3) урон Кислота. Nonmagical armor worn by the target takes a -1 penalty to the AC it offers. The armor is destroyed if the penalty reduces its AC to 10. The penalty can be removed by casting the *Починка* spell on the armor.

### Желатиновый куб

*Большой Слизь, Без мировоззрения*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 6
- **Хиты:** 63 (6d10 + 30)
- **Speed:** 15 фт.
- **Инициатива:** -4 (6)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   14   |   3    |   20   |   1    |   6    |   1    |
|   MOD    |   +2   |   -4   |   +5   |   -5   |   -2   |   -5   |
|   SAVE   |   +2   |   -4   |   +5   |   -5   |   -2   |   -5   |

- **Immunities:** Acid; Ослеплённый, Очарованный, Оглохший, Истощение, Испуганный, Лежащий
- **Чувства:** blindsight 60 фт.; Passive Внимательность 8
- **ПО** 2 (ОО 450; PB +2)

#### Traits

**_Ooze Cube._** The cube fills its entire space and is transparent. Other creatures can enter that space, but a creature that does so is subjected to the cube's Engulf and has Disadvantage on the saving throw.
Creatures inside the cube have Cover|ООHB|Total Cover, and the cube can hold one Большой creature or up to four Средний or Маленький creatures inside itself at a time.
As an action, a creature within 5 feet of the cube can pull a creature or an object out of the cube by succeeding on a DC 12 Сила (Атлетика) check, and the puller takes 10 (3d6) урон Кислота.

**_Transparent._** Even when the cube is in plain sight, a creature must succeed on a DC 15 Мудрость (Внимательность) check to notice the cube if the creature hasn't witnessed the cube move or otherwise act.

#### Действия

**_Pseudopod._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +4, reach 5 фт. 12 (3d6 + 2) урон Кислота.

**_Engulf._** The cube moves up to its Speed without provoking Opportunity Attacks. The cube can move through the spaces of Большой or smaller creatures if it has room inside itself to contain them (see the Слизь Cube [Area of Effect]|ООHB|Cube trait). *Ловкость Saving Throw*: DC 12, each creature whose space the cube enters for the first time during this move. *Failure:* 10 (3d6) урон Кислота, and the target is engulfed. An engulfed target is suffocating, can't cast spells with a Verbal component, has the Опутанный condition, and takes 10 (3d6) урон Кислота at the start of each of the cube's turns. When the cube moves, the engulfed target moves with it. An engulfed target can try to escape by taking an action to make a DC 12 Сила (Атлетика) check. On a successful check, the target escapes and enters the nearest unoccupied space. *Success:* Half damage, and the target moves to an unoccupied space within 5 feet of the cube. If there is no unoccupied space, the target fails the save instead.

### Пурпурный червь

*Громадный Чудовище, Без мировоззрения*

- **Хиты:** 247 (15d20 + 90)
- **Speed:** 50 фт., Burrow 50 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +3 (13)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   28   |   7    |   22   |   1    |   8    |   4    |

- **Чувства:** blindsight 30 фт., tremorsense 60 фт.; Passive Внимательность 9

**_Tunneler._** The worm can рытьё through solid rock at half its Burrow Speed and leaves a 10-foot-diameter tunnel in its wake.

**_Tail Stinger._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +14, reach 10 фт. 16 (2d6 + 9) урон Колющий plus 35 (10d6) урон Яд.

#### Bonus Действия

**_Swallow._** *Сила Saving Throw*: DC 19, one Большой or smaller creature Схваченный by the worm (it can have up to three creatures swallowed at a time). *Failure:* The target is swallowed by the worm, and the Схваченный condition ends. A swallowed creature has the Ослеплённый and Опутанный conditions, has Cover|ООHB|Total Cover against attacks and other effects outside the worm, and takes 17 (5d6) урон Кислота at the start of each of the worm's turns.
If the worm takes 30 damage or more on a single turn from a creature inside it, the worm must succeed on a DC 21 Телосложение saving throw at the end of that turn or regurgitate all swallowed creatures, each of which falls in a space within 5 feet of the worm and has the Лежащий condition. If the worm dies, any swallowed creature no longer has the Опутанный condition and can escape from the corpse using 20 feet of movement, exiting Лежащий.

## Monsters: Priests

### Жрец

|   MOD    |   +4   |   -1   |   +4   |   -2   |   +0   |   -4   |
|   SAVE   |   +4   |   -1   |   +4   |   -2   |   +0   |   -4   |

- **Immunities:** Poison; Очарованный, Истощение, Испуганный, Парализованный, Окаменевший, Отравленный
- **Чувства:** blindsight 10 фт., darkvision 60 фт.; Passive Внимательность 10
- **Языки:** Understands commands given in any language но не может говорить
- **ПО** 7 (ОО 2,900; PB +3)

#### Traits

**_Bound._** The guardian is magically bound to an amulet. While the guardian and its amulet are on the same plane of existence, the amulet's wearer can telepathically call the guardian to travel to it, and the guardian knows the distance and direction to the amulet. If the guardian is within 60 feet of the amulet's wearer, half of any damage the wearer takes (round up) is transferred to the guardian.

**_Regeneration._** The guardian regains 10 Хиты at the start of each of its turns if it has at least 1 Hit Point.

**_Spell Storing._** A spellcaster who wears the guardian's amulet can cause the guardian to store one spell of level 4 or lower. To do so, the wearer must cast the spell on the guardian while within 5 feet of it. The spell has no effect but is stored within the guardian. Any previously stored spell is lost when a new spell is stored. The guardian can cast the spell stored with any parameters set by the original caster, requiring no spell components and using the caster's spellcasting ability. The stored spell is then lost.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The guardian makes two Fist attacks.

**_Fist._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +7, reach 10 фт. 11 (2d6 + 4) урон Дробящий plus 7 (2d6) урон Силовое поле.

- **Хиты:** 22 (5d8)

**_Draining Kiss._** *Телосложение Saving Throw*: DC 15, one creature Очарованный by the succubus within 5 feet. *Failure:* 13 (3d8) урон Психический. *Success:* Half damage. *Failure or Success*: The target's Hit Point maximum decreases by an amount equal to the damage taken.

#### Bonus Действия

**_Shape-Shiфт._** The succubus shape-shifts to resemble a Средний or Маленький Гуманоид or back into its true form. Its game statistics are the same in each form, except its Fly Speed is available only in its true form. Any equipment it's wearing or carrying isn't transformed.

## Monsters: Sphinxes

### Сфинкс знаний

*Большой Небожитель, Принципиально-нейтральный*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 17
- **Хиты:** 170 (20d10 + 60)
- **Speed:** 40 фт., Fly 60 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +6 (16)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   18   |   15   |   16   |   18   |   18   |   18   |
|   MOD    |   +4   |   +2   |   +3   |   +4   |   +4   |   +4   |
|   SAVE   |   +4   |   +2   |   +3   |   +4   |   +4   |   +4   |

- **Resistances:** Necrotic, Radiant
- **Immunities:** Psychic; Очарованный, Испуганный
- **Навыки:** Аркана +12, История +12, Внимательность +8, Религия +12
- **Чувства:** truesight 120 фт.; Passive Внимательность 18
- **Языки:** Небожитель, Общий
- **ПО** 11 (ОО 7,200, or 8,400 in lair)

#### Traits

**_Inscrutable._** No magic can observe the sphinx remotely or detect its thoughts without its permission. Мудрость (Проницательность) checks made to ascertain its intentions or sincerity are made with Disadvantage.

**_Легендарное сопротивление (3/Day, or 4/Day in Lair)._** If the sphinx fails a saving throw, it can choose to succeed instead.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The sphinx makes three Claw attacks.

**_Claw._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +8, reach 5 фт. 14 (3d6 + 4) урон Рубящий.

**_Mind-Rending Roar (Recharge 5-6)._** *Мудрость Saving Throw*: DC 16, each enemy in a 300-foot Emanation originating from the sphinx. *Failure:* 35 (10d6) урон Психический, and the target has the Недееспособный condition until the start of the sphinx's next turn.

**_Использование заклинаний._** The sphinx casts one of the following spells, requiring no Material components and using Интеллект as the spellcasting ability (spell save DC 16):

- **At Will:** *Обнаружение магии*, *Опознание*, *Волшебная рука*, *Малая иллюзия*, *Фокусы*
- **1e/Day Each:** *Рассеивание магии*, *Знание легенд*, *Поиск объекта*, *Переход между планами*, *Снятие проклятия*, *Языки*

#### Legendary Действия

**_Arcane Prowl._** The sphinx can teleport up to 30 feet to an unoccupied space it can see, and it makes one Claw attack.

**_Weight of Years._** *Телосложение Saving Throw*: DC 16, one creature the sphinx can see within 120 feet. *Failure:* The target gains 1 Истощение level. While the target has any Истощение levels, it appears 3d10 years older. *Failure or Success*: The sphinx can't take this action again until the start of its next turn.

### Сфинкс доблести

*Большой Небожитель, Принципиально-нейтральный*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 17
- **Хиты:** 199 (19d10 + 95)
- **Speed:** 40 фт., Fly 60 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +4 (14)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   22   |   10   |   20   |   16   |   23   |   18   |
|   MOD    |   +6   |   +0   |   +5   |   +3   |   +6   |   +4   |
|   SAVE   |   +6   |   +6   |  +11   |   +9   |  +12   |   +4   |

- **Resistances:** Necrotic, Radiant
- **Immunities:** Psychic; Очарованный, Испуганный
- **Навыки:** Аркана +9, Внимательность +12, Религия +15
- **Чувства:** truesight 120 фт.; Passive Внимательность 22
- **Языки:** Небожитель, Общий
- **ПО** 17 (ОО 18,000, or 20,000 in lair)

#### Traits

**_Inscrutable._** No magic can observe the sphinx remotely or detect its thoughts without its permission. Мудрость (Проницательность) checks made to ascertain its intentions or sincerity are made with Disadvantage.

**_Легендарное сопротивление (3/Day, or 4/Day in Lair)._** If the sphinx fails a saving throw, it can choose to succeed instead.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The sphinx makes two Claw attacks and uses Roar.

**_Claw._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +12, reach 5 фт. 20 (4d6 + 6) урон Рубящий.

**_Roar (3/Day)._** The sphinx emits a magical roar. Whenever it roars, the roar has a different effect, as detailed below (the sequence resets when it takes a Long Rest):

- **First Roar:** *Мудрость Saving Throw*: DC 20, each enemy in a 500-foot Emanation originating from the sphinx. *Failure:* The target has the Испуганный condition for 1 minute.
- **Second Roar:** *Мудрость Saving Throw*: DC 20, each enemy in a 500-foot Emanation originating from the sphinx. *Failure:* The target has the Парализованный condition, and it repeats the save at the end of each of its turns, ending the effect on itself on a success. After 1 minute, it succeeds automatically.
- **Third Roar:** *Телосложение Saving Throw*: DC 20, each enemy in a 500-foot Emanation originating from the sphinx. *Failure:* 44 (8d10) урон Гром, and the target has the Лежащий condition. *Success:* Half damage only.

**_Использование заклинаний._** The sphinx casts one of the following spells, requiring no Material components and using Мудрость as the spellcasting ability (spell save DC 20):

- **At Will:** *Обнаружение добра и зла*, *Тауматургия*
- **1e/Day Each:** *Обнаружение магии*, *Рассеивание магии*, *Высшее восстановление*, *Пир героев*, *Зона правды*

#### Legendary Действия

**_Arcane Prowl._** The sphinx can teleport up to 30 feet to an unoccupied space it can see, and it makes one Claw attack.

**_Weight of Years._** *Телосложение Saving Throw*: DC 16, one creature the sphinx can see within 120 feet. *Failure:* The target gains 1 Истощение level. While the target has any Истощение levels, it appears 3d10 years older. *Failure or Success*: The sphinx can't take this action again until the start of its next turn.

*Маленький Небожитель, Принципиально-добрый*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 13
- **Хиты:** 24 (7d4 + 7)
- **Speed:** 20 фт., Fly 40 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +3 (13)

|  SCORE   |   6    |   17   |   13   |   15   |   12   |   11   |

- **Resistances:** Necrotic, Psychic, Radiant
- **Навыки:** Аркана +4, Религия +4, Скрытность +5
- **Чувства:** darkvision 60 фт.; Passive Внимательность 11
- **Языки:** Небожитель, Общий
- **ПО** 1 (ОО 200; PB +2)

#### Traits

## Monsters: T

### Тарраска

- **Класс Доспеха:** 25
- **Хиты:** 697 (34d20 + 340)
- **Speed:** 60 фт., Burrow 40 фт., Climb 60 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +18 (28)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   30   |   11   |   30   |   3    |   11   |   11   |
|   MOD    |  +10   |   +0   |  +10   |   -4   |   +0   |   +0   |
|   SAVE   |  +10   |   +9   |  +10   |   +5   |   +9   |   +9   |

- **Resistances:** Bludgeoning, Piercing, Slashing
- **Immunities:** Fire, Poison; Очарованный, Оглохший, Испуганный, Парализованный, Отравленный
- **Навыки:** Внимательность +9
- **Чувства:** blindsight 120 фт.; Passive Внимательность 19
- **ПО** 30 (ОО 155,000; PB +9)

#### Traits

**_Легендарное сопротивление (6/Day)._** If the tarrasque fails a saving throw, it can choose to succeed instead.

**_Magic Resistance._** The tarrasque has Advantage on saving throws against spells and other magical effects.

**_Reflective Carapace._** If the tarrasque is targeted by a *Магическая стрела* spell or a spell that requires a ranged attack roll, roll 1d6. On a 1-5, the tarrasque is unaffected. On a 6, the tarrasque is unaffected and reflects the spell, turning the caster into the target.

**_Siege Monster._** The tarrasque deals double damage to objects and structures.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The tarrasque makes one Bite attack and three other attacks, using Claw or Tail in any combination.

**_Bite._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +19, reach 15 фт. 36 (4d12 + 10) урон Колющий, and the target has the Схваченный condition (escape DC 20). Until the grapple ends, the target has the Опутанный condition and can't teleport.

**_Claw._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +19, reach 15 фт. 28 (4d8 + 10) урон Рубящий.

**_Tail._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +19, reach 30 фт. 23 (3d8 + 10) урон Дробящий. If the target is a Огромный or smaller creature, it has the Лежащий condition.

**_Thunderous Bellow (Recharge 5-6)._** *Телосложение Saving Throw*: DC 27, each creature and each object that isn't being worn or carried in a 150-foot Cone. *Failure:* 78 (12d12) урон Гром, and the target has the Оглохший and Испуганный conditions until the end of its next turn. *Success:* Half damage only.

#### Bonus Действия

**_Swallow._** *Сила Saving Throw*: DC 27, one Большой or smaller creature Схваченный by the tarrasque (it can have up to six creatures swallowed at a time). *Failure:* The target is swallowed, and the Схваченный condition ends. A swallowed creature has the Ослеплённый and Опутанный conditions and can't teleport, it has Cover|ООHB|Total Cover against attacks and other effects outside the tarrasque, and it takes 56 (16d6) урон Кислота at the start of each of the tarrasque's turns.
If the tarrasque takes 60 damage or more on a single turn from a creature inside it, the tarrasque must succeed on a DC 20 Телосложение saving throw at the end of that turn or regurgitate all swallowed creatures, each of which falls in a space within 10 feet of the tarrasque and has the Лежащий condition. If the tarrasque dies, any swallowed creature no longer has the Опутанный condition and can escape from the corpse using 20 feet of movement, exiting Лежащий.

#### Legendary Действия

**_Onslaught._** The tarrasque moves up to half its Speed, and it makes one Claw or Tail attack.

**_World-Shaking Movement._** The tarrasque moves up to its Speed. At the end of this movement, the tarrasque creates an instantaneous shock wave in a 60-foot Emanation originating from itself. Creatures in that area lose Concentration and, if Средний or smaller, have the Лежащий condition. The tarrasque can't take this action again until the start of its next turn.

The tree takes its turn immediately after the treant on the same Инициатива count, and it obeys the treant. A tree remains animate for 1 day or until it dies, the treant dies, or it is more than 120 feet from the treant. The tree then takes root if possible.
