## Monsters: Vampires

### Вампир

*Маленький Нежить, Принципиально-злой*

- **Класс Доспеха:** 16
- **Хиты:** 195 (23d8 + 92)
- **Speed:** 40 фт., Climb 40 фт.
- **Инициатива:** +8 (18)

|          |  СИЛ   |  ЛОВ   |  ТЕЛ   |  ИНТ   |  МДР   |  ХАР   |
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
|  SCORE   |   18   |   18   |   18   |   17   |   15   |   18   |
|   MOD    |   +4   |   +4   |   +4   |   +3   |   +2   |   +4   |
|   SAVE   |   +4   |   +9   |   +9   |   +3   |   +7   |   +9   |

- **Resistances:** Necrotic
- **Навыки:** Внимательность +7, Скрытность +9
- **Чувства:** darkvision 120 фт.; Passive Внимательность 17
- **Языки:** Общий plus two other languages
- **ПО** 13 (ОО 10,000, or 11,500 in lair)

#### Traits

**_Легендарное сопротивление (3/Day, or 4/Day in Lair)._** If the vampire fails a saving throw, it can choose to succeed instead.

**_Misty Escape._** If the vampire drops to 0 Хиты outside its resting place, the vampire uses Shape-Shift to become mist (no action required). If it can't use Shape-Shift, it is destroyed.
While it has 0 Хиты in mist form, it can't return to its vampire form, and it must reach its resting place within 2 hours or be destroyed. Once in its resting place, it returns to its vampire form and has the Парализованный condition until it regains any Хиты, and it regains 1 Hit Point after spending 1 hour there.

**_Spider Climb._** The vampire can climb difficult surfaces, including along ceilings, without needing to make an ability check.

**_Vampire Weakness._** The vampire has these weaknesses:

- **Forbiddance:** The vampire can't enter a residence without an invitation from an occupant.
- **Running Water:** The vampire takes 20 урон Кислота if it ends its turn in running water.
- **Stake to the Heart:** If a weapon that deals урон Колющий is driven into the vampire's heart while the vampire has the Недееспособный condition in its resting place, the vampire has the Парализованный condition until the weapon is removed.
- **Sunlight:** The vampire takes 20 урон Излучение if it starts its turn in sunlight. While in sunlight, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls and ability checks.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака (Vampire Form Only)._** The vampire makes two Grave Strike attacks and uses Bite.

**_Grave Strike (Vampire Form Only)._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +9, reach 5 фт. 8 (1d8 + 4) урон Дробящий plus 7 (2d6) урон Некротический. If the target is a Большой or smaller creature, it has the Схваченный condition (escape DC 14) from one of two hands.

**_Bite (Bat or Vampire Form Only)._** *Телосложение Saving Throw*: DC 17, one creature within 5 feet that is willing or that has the Схваченный, Недееспособный, or Опутанный condition. *Failure:* 6 (1d4 + 4) урон Колющий plus 13 (3d8) урон Некротический. The target's Hit Point maximum decreases by an amount equal to the урон Некротический taken, and the vampire regains Хиты equal to that amount. A Гуманоид reduced to 0 Хиты by this damage and then buried rises the following sunset as a Vampire Spawn under the vampire's control.

#### Bonus Действия

**_Shape-Shiфт._** If the vampire isn't in sunlight or running water, it shape-shifts into a Крошечный bat (Speed 5 фт., Fly Speed 30 фт.) or a Средний cloud of mist (Speed 5 фт., Fly Speed 20 фт. [hover]), or it returns to its vampire form. Anything it is wearing transforms with it.
While in bat form, the vampire can't speak. Its game statistics, other than its size and Speed, are unchanged.
While in mist form, the vampire can't take any actions, speak, or manipulate objects. It is weightless and can enter an enemy's space and stop there. If air can pass through a space, the mist can do so, but it can't pass through liquid. It has Resistance to all damage, except the damage it takes from sunlight.

**_Charm (Recharge 5-6)._** The vampire casts *Очарование личности*, requiring no spell components and using Харизма as the spellcasting ability (spell save DC 17), and the duration is 24 hours. The Очарованный target is a willing recipient of the vampire's Bite, the damage of which doesn't end the spell. When the spell ends, the target is unaware it was Очарованный by the vampire.

#### Legendary Действия

**_Deathless Strike._** The vampire moves up to half its Speed, and it makes one Grave Strike attack.

**_Beguile._** The vampire casts *Приказ*, requiring no spell components and using Харизма as the spellcasting ability (spell save DC 17). The vampire can't take this action again until the start of its next turn.

- **Forbiddance:** The vampire can't enter a residence without an invitation from an occupant.
- **Running Water:** The vampire takes 20 урон Кислота if it ends its turn in running water.
- **Stake to the Heart:** The vampire is destroyed if a weapon that deals урон Колющий is driven into the vampire's heart while the vampire has the Недееспособный condition.
- **Sunlight:** The vampire takes 20 урон Излучение if it starts its turn in sunlight. While in sunlight, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls and ability checks.

#### Действия

**_Мультиатака._** The vampire makes two Claw attacks and uses Bite.

**_Claw._** *Бросок рукопашной атаки:* +6, reach 5 фт. 8 (2d4 + 3) урон Рубящий. If the target is a Средний or smaller creature, it has the Схваченный condition (escape DC 13) from one of two claws.

**_Bite._** *Телосложение Saving Throw*: DC 14, one creature within 5 feet that is willing or that has the Схваченный, Недееспособный, or Опутанный condition. *Failure:* 5 (1d4 + 3) урон Колющий plus 10 (3d6) урон Некротический. The target's Hit Point maximum decreases by an amount equal to the урон Некротический taken, and the vampire regains Хиты equal to that amount.

#### Bonus Действия

**_Deathless Agility._** The vampire takes the Dash or Disengage action.
